The referer is empty.\n162:         if not referer:\n163:             return True\n164: \n165:         # APPEND_SLASH is enabled and the referer is equal to the current URL\n166:         # without a trailing slash indicating an internal redirect.\n167:         if settings.APPEND_SLASH and uri.endswith(\"/\") and referer == uri[:-1]:\n168:             return True\n169: \n170:         # RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: maximum requests per window (default: 100)\n    - RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: time window in seconds (default: 3600)\n\n    Returns an HTTP 403 response when the rate limit is exceeded.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, get_response):\n        super().__init__(get_response)\n        self.rate_limit_requests = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS\", 100)\n        self.rate_limit_window = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW\", 3600)\n        # Dictionary to track request timestamps per IP address\n        self.request_tracker = {}\n        # Counter for cleanup operations\n        self.request_count = 0\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract the client IP address from the request.\n\n        Checks X-Forwarded-For header first (for proxied requests),\n        then falls back to REMOTE_ADDR.\n        \"\"\"\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get(\"HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR\")\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            # X-Forwarded-For can contain multiple IPs; take the first one\n            return x_forwarded_for.split(\",\")[0].strip()\n        return request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Remove expired entries from the request tracker.\n\n        This is called periodically to prevent the tracker from growing\n        indefinitely.\n        \"\"\"\n        current_time = time.time()\n        expired_ips = []\n\n        for ip, timestamps in self.request_tracker.items():\n            # Remove timestamps outside the window\n            valid_timestamps = [\n                ts for ts in timestamps if current_time - ts < self.rate_limit_window\n            ]\n            if valid_timestamps:\n                self.request_tracker[ip] = valid_timestamps\n            else:\n                expired_ips.append(ip)\n\n        # Remove IPs with no valid timestamps\n        for ip in expired_ips:\n            del self.request_tracker[ip]\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n\n        Returns an HTTP 403 response if the limit is exceeded.\n        \"\"\"\n        client_ip = self.get_client_ip(request)\n        current_time = time.time()\n\n        # Perform cleanup every 100 requests\n        self.request_count += 1\n        if self.request_count >= 100:\n            self.cleanup_expired_entries()\n            self.request_count = 0\n\n        # Initialize tracker for this IP if not present\n        if client_ip not in self.request_tracker:\n            self.request_tracker[client_ip] = []\n\n        # Remove timestamps outside the current window\n        valid_timestamps = [\n            ts\n            for ts in self.request_tracker[client_ip]\n            if current_time - ts < self.rate_limit_window\n            ]\n            if valid_timestamps:\n                self.request_tracker[ip] = valid_timestamps\n            else:\n                expired_ips.append(ip)\n\n        # Remove IPs with no valid timestamps\n        for ip in expired_ips:\n            del self.request_tracker[ip]\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n\n        Returns an HTTP 403 response if the limit is exceeded.\n        \"\"\"\n        client_ip = self.get_client_ip(request)\n        current_time = time.time()\n\n        # Perform cleanup every 100 requests\n        self.request_count += 1\n        if self.request_count >= 100:\n            self.cleanup_expired_entries()\n            self.request_count = 0\n\n        # Initialize tracker for this IP if not present\n        if client_ip not in self.request_tracker:\n            self.request_tracker[client_ip] = []\n\n        # Remove timestamps outside the current window\n        valid_timestamps = [\n            ts\n            for ts in self.request_tracker[client_ip]\n            if current_time - RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: maximum requests per window (default: 100)\n    - RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: time window in seconds (default: 3600)\n\n    Returns an HTTP 403 response when the rate limit is exceeded.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, get_response):\n        super().__init__(get_response)\n        self.rate_limit_requests = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS\", 100)\n        self.rate_limit_window = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW\", 3600)\n        # Dictionary to track request timestamps per IP address\n        self.request_tracker = {}\n        # Counter for cleanup operations\n        self.request_count = 0\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract the client IP address from the request.\n\n        Checks X-Forwarded-For header first (for proxied requests),\n        then falls back to REMOTE_ADDR.\n        \"\"\"\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get(\"HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR\")\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            # X-Forwarded-For can contain multiple IPs; take the first one\n            return x_forwarded_for.split(\",\")[0].strip()\n        return request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"\")\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Remove expired entries from the request tracker.\n\n        This is called periodically to prevent the tracker from growing\n        indefinitely.\n        \"\"\"\n        current_time = time.time()\n        expired_ips = []\n\n        for ip, timestamps in self.request_tracker.items():\n            # Remove timestamps outside the window\n            valid_timestamps = [\n                ts for ts in timestamps if current_time - ts < self.rate_limit_window\n            ]\n            if valid_timestamps:\n                self.request_tracker[ip] = valid_timestamps\n            else:\n                expired_ips.append(ip)\n\n        # Remove IPs with no valid timestamps\n        for ip in expired_ips:\n            del self.request_tracker[ip]\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client has exceeded the rate limit.\n\n        Returns an HTTP 403 response if the limit is exceeded.\n        \"\"\"\n        client_ip = self.get_client_ip(request)\n        current_time = time.time()\n\n        # Perform cleanup every 100 requests\n        self.request_count += 1\n        if self.request_count >= 100:\n            self.cleanup_expired_entries()\n            self.request_count = 0\n\n        # Initialize tracker for this IP if not present\n        if client_ip not in self.request_tracker:\n            self.request_tracker[client_ip] = []\n\n        # Remove timestamps outside the current window\n        valid_timestamps = [\n            ts\n            for ts in self.request_tracker[client_ip]\n            if current_time - ts < self.rate_limit_window\n        ]\n        self.request_tracker[client_ip] = valid_timestamps\n\n        # Check if limit exceeded\n        if len(valid_timestamps) >= self.rate_limit_requests:\n            return HttpResponseForbidden(\n                f\"Rate limit exceeded for IP {client_ip}\"\n            )\n\n        # Record this request\n        self.request_tracker[client_ip].append(current_time)\n\n        return None\n","numLines":109,"startLine":1,"totalLines":109}}}
